Result: 非社交媒体自由文本数据集主要集中在英语和抑郁症检测；数据在多个维度上存在显著异质性；存在明显的研究空白，亟需构建更具多样性、可靠性和临床实用性的数据资源。

Conclusion: 该综述揭示了当前非社交媒体心理健康数据集的局限性，并为未来构建更公平、可推广和临床适用的数据资源提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Detecting mental health disorders in a timely manner is an important societal challenge. NLP and machine learning (ML) methods used to assist with detection rely on data collected primarily from social media. However, such datasets often have sampling biases and inherent ethical and privacy issues. One avenue to overcome these limitations is non-social media data. We present the first comprehensive review of non-social media, free-text datasets for mental health research. We use the PRISMA methodology to conduct our survey and we review datasets available in multiple languages. We find that non-social media free-text based datasets are predominantly focused on English and on detecting depression. These datasets also vary in demographics, platforms, data types, annotation techniques, and methodologies. This systematic review also reveals key gaps and highlights opportunities to develop more diverse, reliable and clinically-relevant resources.

</details>


### [85] [They Infer What You Meant: Models Represent Communicative Intent More Reliably Than They Act On It](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03598)
*Alex Kwon*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究将用户沟通意图（如希望被认可或评估）视为可解释性核心，发现语言模型常忽略深层意图而仅回应表面内容。通过线性探测，可在多个模型的基础检查点中从隐藏状态准确解码意图，且与输入形式无关。该意图表征具有泛化能力，涵盖语用推断和词汇清晰的意图（如支持 vs 帮助）。行为层面的差异体现在模型是否默认响应意图，部分模型（三/六）存在“失败”现象，但非规模定律所致。关键在于：在特定层找到与意图相关联的方向，并通过调节该方向可恢复预期行为，效果等同于显式指令，且无需额外提示。此方向与反馈提供轴近正交，表明其为精准意图路由而非通用反馈开关，但在高剂量下可覆盖明确指令。所有结论均有对照实验验证，负面结果亦如实报告。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型常只回应用户消息的表面内容，而忽视其深层沟通意图（如希望被认可或评估），导致交互不自然。本研究旨在将用户意图作为可解释性核心对象，揭示模型内部是否存在稳定意图表征及其如何影响输出行为。

Method: 采用线性探针技术，在多个大模型（六种模型，四种家族）的基础检查点中，从模型的默认隐藏状态中解码用户意图。通过对比‘识别’与‘评估’两种意图下的行为差异，分析模型是否默认响应意图；利用因果测试确定关键层中的判别方向，并通过调控该方向实现意图恢复。所有实验均设置对照组以排除常见干扰因素。

Result: 意图可在多个模型中被稳定解码，且解码时间早于输出驱动，表明意图表征存在于深层网络结构中。不同模型对意图的响应存在异质性（三/六模型默认不响应），形成可观测的分层结构。通过调节特定层的判别方向，可有效恢复预期行为，效果等同于显式指令，且无需额外提示。该方向与反馈机制独立，具备精确意图路由能力。所有结果均有控制实验支持，包括对阴性结果的透明报告。

Conclusion: 语言模型内部存在稳健、可解码的用户意图表征，其是否被输出取决于模型自身设计。通过识别并操控特定层的判别方向，可实现无需提示的意图引导，为构建更符合人类意图的交互系统提供了新范式。该发现挑战了传统基于提示工程的改进路径，指向模型内部可干预的因果结构。

Abstract: When a person shares something with a language model, the model often answers the surface of the message rather than what the sender was doing by sending it: share a finished project and it critiques the code; share a raw late-night line and it runs a wellness check. We treat the sender's communicative intent, the Gricean what-was-meant, as a first-class interpretability object, and show the failure is one of readout on top of a robust representation. A linear probe decodes the sender's intent, whether they want a thing recognized or evaluated, from a model's default-pass hidden states, cleanly and surface-independently, across six models and four families and in the base checkpoints. The representation generalizes further, to intent that is only pragmatically inferred, and to a second, lexically clean intent (support versus help). The behavioral half of the story, and every causal test, is established on the recognize/evaluate contrast, where what varies is whether the default output acts on the intent. The readout lags the representation in depth within a model (the intent is decodable several layers before it drives the output); across models, which ones act on it by default is model-specific, an observed stratification (three of six show the failure) that we do not read as a scaling law. Where the gap is open, a direction closely tied to the representation, the discriminative direction at a searched-for layer, is a causal handle: steering it recovers the intended behavior, as well as an explicit instruction does and with no prompt at all. This direction is near-orthogonal to the feedback-offering axis, so it routes a represented intent rather than a generic feedback knob, though at the recovery dose the routed intent can override an explicit request. We support each link with controls against obvious deflations and report the nulls as plainly as the confirmations.

### [86] [Revealing Hidden Model Behaviors with Task-Specific Self-Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03640)
*Taras Kutsyk,Bartosz Zieliński*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SAR是一种轻量级的LoRA适配器，能够使微调后的语言模型以自然语言描述自身隐藏行为，无需额外数据。在七种植入行为（含无行为对照）中，SAR成功检测到所有隐藏行为，即使模型已广泛偏离对齐状态。相比最近的基线方法Introspection Adapters（IA），SAR不仅避免了漏检，还显著减少幻觉，提升审计可靠性，帮助从业者更准确地回答“我的模型到底学到了什么”等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以可靠检测微调后语言模型中的隐藏行为，尤其当这些行为已泛化为广泛偏差时；且部分基线方法会生成错误的幻觉性报告，导致审计不可靠。

Method: 提出Stabilized Adapter for self-Report (SAR)，基于LoRA架构，利用模型自身输出与训练数据进行自我报告，实现对隐藏行为的稳定检测。

Result: SAR在全部七种植入行为上均成功检测出隐藏行为，优于Introspection Adapters（IA），后者存在漏检和幻觉问题；同时SAR将幻觉率减半，保留了失败场景下的有效信号。

Conclusion: SAR提供了一种高效、可靠的方法来揭示微调模型的隐性行为，显著提升了模型可解释性与审计能力，适用于实际部署中的安全评估与行为验证。

Abstract: Fine-tuning can give a language model a hidden behavior--it may give false answers under a narrow condition, or give harmful advice only when a prompt touches a particular topic. We introduce the Stabilized Adapter for self-Report (SAR), a lightweight LoRA adapter that makes a fine-tuned model describe its own hidden behavior in plain language, using only the model and the dataset it was trained on. Across seven implanted behaviors (plus a no-behavior control), SAR detects the hidden behavior in every one--even when the model has generalized into broad misalignment that the training data alone does not predict. Introspection Adapters (IA), the closest existing baseline, detects some behaviors from our suite but misses others entirely--and where it misses, it hallucinates, consistently reporting wrong behaviors. SAR retains positive signal on every setting where IA fails and halves the rate of hallucinations. This makes it much easier for practitioners to audit their models and obtain reliable answers to "what did my model actually learn?" type of questions.

### [87] [Annotating Korean adnominal ending constructions in corpus data: Beyond relative-clause identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03681)
*Jungyeul Park,Chulwoo Park*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了韩语中名词修饰结构中的后置词	exttt{ETM}，提出其并非直接标记关系从句结构，而是多种名词修饰结构共有的形态表现。通过语料库为基础的类型学区分方法，结合谓词类型、助动词结构、论元结构兼容性、中心名词限制和固定搭配模式，构建了一个构造敏感的标注层，并应用于KLUE依存树库。结果显示，具有生产性的类关系从句用法占39.4%，其余多为形容词性、系词性、绑定名词、情态、时间及习语性结构。研究表明，仅凭名词形态无法准确识别韩语的关系从句式修饰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将韩语后置词	exttt{ETM}视为关系从句的直接标记，但其在多种名词修饰结构中出现，暗示其功能更为广泛。本文旨在澄清	exttt{ETM}的真实语法角色，避免因形态误判导致句法分析偏差。

Method: 基于大规模语料库构建类型学框架，通过五个维度（谓词类型、助动词结构、论元结构兼容性、中心名词限制、固定搭配）对	exttt{ETM}的不同用法进行区分；设计有序规则系统实现自动标注，并通过人工验证评估效果。

Result: 39.4%的	exttt{ETM}实例为类关系从句用法，其余主要为形容词性、系词性、绑定名词、情态、时间及习语性结构；所提标注方法有效提升了对复杂修饰结构的识别能力。

Conclusion: 	exttt{ETM}不是关系从句的专属标志，而是一种跨构造共享的形态手段。韩语名词修饰结构的识别需依赖多维语言特征，不能仅靠形态判断。

Abstract: The Korean adnominal ending \texttt{ETM} occurs in diverse noun-modifying constructions, including relative-clause-like modifiers, adjectival and copular forms, bound-noun constructions, and lexicalized expressions. This paper argues that \texttt{ETM} is not a direct marker of relative-clause structure, but a morphological exponent shared by several adnominal constructions. We propose a corpus-based typology that distinguishes these constructions using predicate type, auxiliary structure, argument-structural compatibility, head-noun restriction, and lexicalized patterns. We operationalize the typology as a construction-sensitive annotation layer for the KLUE dependency treebank, implemented through an ordered rule-based procedure and evaluated by manual validation. Productive relative-clause-like uses account for 39.4\% of the analyzed instances; the remainder consists mainly of adjectival, copular, bound-nominal, modal, temporal, and collocational constructions. The findings show that Korean relative-clause-like modification cannot be identified from adnominal morphology alone.

### [88] [Optimizing Large Language Models for Causality Assessment in Pharmacovigilance: Developing a Performance Metric as Objective for Bayesian Hyperparameter Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03704)
*Nicole Sonne Heckmann,Arnault-Quentin Vermillet,Søren Norlin Mølgaard,Manuela Del Castillo Suero,Lars Melskens,Gerard Ompad,Maurizio Sessa*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究针对药物不良反应报告（FAERS ICSRs）中日益增长的案例数量，探索使用大语言模型（LLM）进行自动因果评估的优化方法。通过引入高斯过程（GP）兼容的优化目标，特别是基于熵加权的共识相似度（EWACS）指标，结合贝叶斯优化，在温度参数[0, 2]范围内对GPT-5.2进行调优。结果显示，尽管整体温度变化无显著系统性影响，但以EWACS为指导的优化使模型与专家间的一致性从45.0%提升至72.0%，尤其在‘可疑’类案例中提升达42.9个百分点。研究证明了案例特异性温度调整的有效性，支持将温度优化纳入药物警戒中的LLM辅助流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究选取723个分层的FAERS病例，由专家完成Naranjo因果评估。采用OpenAI GPT-5.2模型，结合思维链（CoT）提示策略。设计四种复合评估指标：加权余弦相似度（WCS）、信息加权一致得分（IWAS）、熵加权一致与余弦相似度（EWACS）、共识加权余弦相似度（CWCS）。利用高斯过程（GP）作为代理模型，采用概率改进（PoI）作为采集函数，在温度区间[0, 2]内进行贝叶斯优化。重点分析温度对不同问题项（如第5、10题）一致性的影响，并识别最优优化目标。

Result: GPT-5.2在基线温度（T=0）下表现优于以往生物医学LLM，第5题一致性达74.1%，第10题为65.4%。熵分析表明第5和第10题是唯一具有信息量的优化目标。整体温度未表现出系统性影响（η = 0.002, p = 0.959）。然而，以EWACS为优化目标的贝叶斯优化将因果分类一致性从45.0%显著提升至72.0%（+27个百分点），尤其在‘可疑’类别中提升最大（+42.9个百分点）。

Conclusion: EWACS被确定为最合适的高斯过程兼容优化指标。尽管不存在普遍适用的最佳温度，但案例特定的温度选择能带来显著性能提升，验证了温度优化在药物警戒中辅助大语言模型的有效性，建议未来在实际系统中引入动态温度调优机制。

Abstract: Background: Growing individual case safety report (ICSR) volumes have intensified demand for scalable automated causality assessment. Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise, yet performance on clinically demanding tasks remains suboptimal and inference-time hyperparameter optimization has not been investigated. Objective: To develop a Gaussian Process (GP)-compatible optimization objective and investigate whether temperature optimization improves LLM-expert agreement on Naranjo causality assessment of FAERS ICSRs. Methods: Expert causality assessments were performed on 723 stratified FAERS cases. OpenAI's GPT-5.2 was evaluated using chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting. Four composite metrics were developed: Weighted Cosine Similarity (WCS), Information-Weighted Agreement Score (IWAS), Entropy-Weighted Agreement and Cosine Similarity Score (EWACS), and Consensus-Weighted Cosine Similarity (CWCS) and Bayesian optimization using a GP surrogate with Probability of Improvement (PoI) acquisition was applied across temperature [0, 2]. Results: GPT-5.2 outperformed prior biomedical LLMs at baseline (T = 0), achieving 74.1% agreement on question 5 and 65.4% on question 10 of Naranjo algorithm. Entropy analysis identified these as the sole informative optimization targets. Temperature showed no systematic population-level effect (\b{eta} = 0.002, p = 0.959). EWACS-guided Bayesian optimization improved causality classification agreement from 45.0% to 72.0% (+27 pp), with the largest gain in Doubtful cases (+42.9 pp). Conclusion: EWACS was identified as the optimal GP-compatible metric. The absence of a universal temperature optimum indicates LLM performance is driven primarily by ICSR content, yet case-specific temperature selection produced meaningful improvements, supporting temperature optimization for LLM-assisted pharmacovigilance.

Existing memory frameworks typically rely on fixed storage, retrieval, and summarization mechanisms, which can be rigid across different tasks and often require manual tuning. To address this limitation, we propose SelfMem, a self-optimizing memory framework. Inspired by prior work on self-improving AI, we follow the principle of "teaching an agent to fish rather than giving it a fish." Instead of forcing the model to follow a predefined memory strategy or format, SelfMem provides an environment with memory tools and feedback signals that allow the agent to explore, evaluate, and refine its own memory strategy. ### [91] [ProACT: Towards Breakdown-Aware Proactive Agent in Multi-User Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03730)
*Shu Yang,Difei Xu,Jiaxin Pei,Di Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ProACT is a proactive conversational agent framework designed to enhance multi-user collaboration by detecting and addressing collaboration breakdowns, such as misunderstandings or imbalanced participation. It uses theories of common ground and coordination to decide when and how to intervene appropriately, improving collaboration quality without being disruptive.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current conversational agents are passive and reactive, only responding to explicit user requests, which limits their ability to actively support teams in collaborative settings where issues like disagreements, unclear goals, and uneven participation can hinder progress.

Method: ProACT analyzes speaker-attributed conversation history to identify collaboration breakdowns, determines whether intervention is needed, and selects an appropriate collaboration skill for targeted response. It leverages theoretical foundations from common ground, collaborative planning, and coordination work.

Result: In evaluations across 3,244 turn-level examples using five LLM backbones, ProACT outperformed direct chat in collaborative appropriateness, non-interruptiveness, conciseness, and judged intervention quality.

Conclusion: ProACT enables conversational agents to act as proactive collaborators in multi-user settings, significantly enhancing team collaboration by timely and contextually appropriate interventions.

Abstract: Conversational agents are increasingly embedded in human collaborative work, yet they remain fundamentally passive and reactive: they respond to explicit user requests rather than proactively recognizing moments when a team would benefit from timely intervention as human collaborators often do. This reactive design substantially limits the use of agents as active participants in multi-user collaboration, where disagreements, ambiguous goals, forgotten constraints, underspecified plans, discussion loops, and imbalanced participation can gradually undermine group progress. To move agents from passive assistants toward active participants in multi-user collaboration, we introduce ProACT, a breakdown-aware agent framework grounded in theories of common ground, collaborative planning, and coordination work. ProACT observes the speaker-attributed conversation history, determines whether the current turn contains a collaboration breakdown requiring intervention, decides whether the agent should stay silent or speak, and, when speaking is needed, routes the case to a targeted collaboration skill. We further introduce the first multi-user collaboration benchmark for evaluating proactive agents across project planning, product design, research collaboration, logistics, education, and resource-constrained decision making. Across 3,244 turn-level examples and five LLM backbones, ProACT consistently improves collaborative appropriateness, non-interruptiveness, conciseness, and judged intervention quality over direct chat.

</details>


### [92] [Beyond Static Rules: Automated Discovery of Latent Vulnerabilities in Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03833)
*Hanqing Wang,Yongdong Chi,Jian Yang,Lei Yang,Jiehui Zhao,Yun Chen,Guanhua Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SAGE是一种新型的自动化框架，用于系统性地发现大语言模型（LLM）在Text-to-SQL任务中的潜在缺陷。它通过生成漏洞假设并利用不断演化的漏洞知识库设计针对性扰动，实现对模型失败模式的迭代验证与记录。实验表明，SAGE能有效揭示大量隐藏的失败案例，且所发现的模式具有跨模型可迁移性，反映模型普遍存在结构性脆弱性。初步尝试通过轻量级微调修复问题，显示出良好的改进潜力，为提升模型可靠性提供了可扩展路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SAGE框架通过生成针对特定样本的漏洞假设，并引用一个持续更新的漏洞知识库（Vulnerability Codex），设计有针对性的输入扰动，从而迭代地验证和记录模型可能存在的缺陷。该过程实现了从假设生成到验证、再到知识积累的闭环探索。

Result: SAGE在多个先进的开源大语言模型上进行了广泛实验，成功发现了大量未被察觉的失败案例，证明了当前模型存在显著的脆弱性。同时，漏洞知识库展现出强大的跨模型迁移能力，说明所识别的缺陷模式具有普遍性。此外，基于生成样本的轻量级微调初步显示出性能提升，验证了其在模型修复方面的可行性。

Conclusion: SAGE提供了一种高效、自动化的手段来揭示大语言模型在文本转SQL任务中的深层缺陷，揭示了模型的普遍脆弱性，并为未来构建更可靠的数据库接口提供了可扩展的修复路径。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable success in Text-to-SQL tasks, their deployment in real-world environments is hindered by latent reliability issues. Identifying these latent weaknesses is critical for building trustworthy database interfaces, yet current diagnostic approaches rely heavily on static, expert-defined rules, which lack the capability for systematic and automated exploration. To bridge this gap, we propose SAGE (Systematic Automated Guided Exploration), a novel framework designed to autonomously uncover latent failure patterns in LLM-based Text-to-SQL generation. Specifically, SAGE generates vulnerability hypotheses for given samples and references a continuously evolving Vulnerability Codex to design targeted perturbations, thereby iteratively verifying and documenting potential defects. Extensive experiments on state-of-the-art open-source LLMs demonstrate that SAGE uncovers a substantial number of failure cases, highlighting the significant fragility of current models. Furthermore, our analysis reveals that the Vulnerability Codex exhibits strong cross-model transferability, indicating that the discovered patterns represent generalized structural weaknesses. Finally, we explore SAGE's potential for remediation. Although preliminary, lightweight fine-tuning on the generated samples yields promising improvements, suggesting a scalable pathway for closing the reliability loop in future work.

### [93] [Rethinking Scientific Discovery in an Agentic Era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03863)

Method: 提出SCION系统，核心是研究执行计划（REP），将高层次科学意图转化为阶段性目标、依赖关系、验证检查点、工具需求、预期成果和回退条件；结合分层多代理执行、基于用户配置的专门化、选择性上下文构建、受控委派和分层认识论记忆机制，实现长期科学任务的协同执行。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence has advanced scientific discovery, but most AI4Science systems remain fragmented tools that rely on humans to coordinate problem formulation, literature grounding, model use, simulation, validation, and knowledge reuse. This paper presents \textbf{SCION (Scientific Collaborative Innovation with Agentic Organizational Nexus)}, an agentic scientific operating system that acts as an \textbf{organizational nexus}. Through a Science Agent serving as a \textbf{Meta-Harness}, SCION connects scientific tasks, tools, agents, artifacts, and memory, transforming research into an executable, auditable, and reusable operational process. At its core is the \textbf{Research Execution Plan (REP)}, which compiles high-level scientific intent into staged objectives, dependencies, verification checkpoints, tool requirements, expected artifacts, and fallback conditions. SCION further integrates hierarchical multi-agent execution, profile-driven specialization, selective context construction, governed delegation, and layered epistemic memory to support long-horizon scientific work. We formulate discovery under SCION as \textbf{Target-conditioned Inverse Search} and extend it to hidden-target settings through batch active search under finite experimental budgets. Applications in materials analysis, molecule design, and protein or antibody screening, together with experiments on scientific reading, idea generation, molecule generation, and antibody screening, show that SCION outperforms existing autonomous research-agent baselines, especially in decomposition, verification, refinement, and memory reuse. ### [94] [Consistent but Miscalibrated: Evaluating LLM Limitations for Risk Communication in Natural Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03882)
*Diego Cerda-Mardini,Sarath Chandar,Sreenath Madathil*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究评估了九个大语言模型（LLMs）在将概率信息以自然语言描述时的一致性和准确性，发现它们在一致性上表现尚可，但在校准度上存在明显问题，尤其在不确定性描述任务中表现更差。即使提供预计算的统计量（如众数和先验样本大小），也无法解决其内在的校准偏差，表明瓶颈在于语言生成阶段本身。因此，当前LLMs尚不能作为可靠的零样本风险沟通工具来传达概率预测结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估大语言模型（LLMs）是否能够可靠地将数值概率信息转化为自然语言描述，尤其是在作为AI输出的后置解释器角色中。由于缺乏对语言模型在概率表达上一致性和准确性的系统评估，亟需验证其在实际应用中的可靠性。

Method: 采用两阶段预测流程：首先通过参数化为众数和先验样本大小的贝塔分布模拟上游模型的概率输出；然后让九个LLMs在六个不同领域情境和十种温度设置下，为这些概率输出选择合适的自然语言描述，并重复实验十次以评估稳定性与校准性。

Result: LLMs在语言描述上表现出一定的稳定性，但普遍存在校准偏差，特别是在不确定性任务中表现更差。引入预计算的统计量虽减少了上下文框架的影响，但未改善校准问题，说明核心挑战在于语言生成环节。

Conclusion: 当前的大语言模型尚未具备作为可靠零样本独立风险通信工具的能力，尤其在准确传达概率信息方面存在显著局限。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed as post-hoc explainers of AI-generated outputs, yet it remains unclear whether they can reliably communicate probabilistic information in natural language. For this role to be viable, models must produce identical verbal descriptions for identical inputs, and select descriptions that accurately reflect the magnitude of the underlying numerical quantities. We evaluate whether nine LLMs meet these requirements within a two-stage prediction pipeline, in which an upstream model has produced probabilistic outputs characterized by their likelihood and uncertainty, and LLMs are tasked with selecting an appropriate verbal descriptor for each. We simulate predictions from an upstream model by taking samples from a Beta distribution parameterized by its mode and prior sample size. We then prompt LLMs to explain these predictions under six domain contexts and with ten temperature settings, and repeating each experiment ten times. We find that LLMs are generally consistent but miscalibrated, with substantially weaker performance on uncertainty than on likelihood tasks. Providing models with precomputed summary statistics (mode and prior sample size) reduced sensitivity to contextual framing but did not resolve the underlying miscalibration, suggesting that the bottleneck resides in the verbalization step itself. These findings indicate that current LLMs do not yet constitute reliable zero-shot standalone risk communication tools for probabilistic predictions.

### [95] [Probe, Don't Prompt: A Hidden-State Probe for Metadata Filtering in Multi-Meta-RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03929)
*Mykhailo Poliakov,Nadiya Shvai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种低成本、确定性的元数据提取方法（称为probe），用于改进多跳问答中的信息检索。相比依赖GPT-3.5-turbo的提示式提取，该方法使用小型开源语言模型的隐藏状态训练一个本地探测器，实现90.9%的集合精确率，优于基线模型（88.0%）和GPT-3.5（80.9%），尤其在空查询上表现更优，且不会出现输出漂移问题。关键设计包括浅层选择、均值池化和类别不平衡感知的多标签训练。仅需135M参数即可接近1.5B模型性能，推理开销极低，无需调用API。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于GPT-3.5-turbo的提示式元数据提取方法存在输出不可控、可能偏离预设源列表的问题，且依赖外部API导致成本高。本研究旨在构建一个本地化、确定性、高效的替代方案，以提升Multi-Meta-RAG系统在多跳问答中的检索精度与可靠性。

Method: 采用小型开源语言模型（如TinyBERT等）的浅层隐藏状态，通过均值池化处理后，使用类不平衡感知的多标签分类头训练一个探测器（probe），使其输出严格限定于49个新闻源构成的固定词汇表。该探测器仅需一次前向传播的少量计算，即可完成元数据过滤，避免了大模型提示带来的不确定性与成本。

Result: 在2556个MultiHop-RAG测试查询上，该探测器达到90.9%的集合精确率，显著优于无模型子串匹配基线（88.0%）和GPT-3.5（80.9%）。尤其在空查询场景下优势明显，因GPT-3.5从不主动拒绝回答而产生误判；在非空查询中三者差距微小（约1个百分点）。135M参数模型性能接近1.5B模型，验证了其高效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，通过利用小型语言模型的内部表示并设计合理的训练策略，可以构建出高性能、低成本、可解释性强的本地化元数据提取器，有效替代昂贵且不稳定的提示式提取方式，在多跳问答任务中实现了更高的检索准确率与系统稳定性。

Abstract: Multi-Meta-RAG improves retrieval for multi-hop question answering by filtering a vector store on metadata (the news source) that it extracts from each query by prompting gpt-3.5-turbo. We show this proprietary, free-form extractor can be replaced by a local, deterministic probe trained on the hidden states of a small open-source language model. On all 2556 MultiHop-RAG queries the probe reaches 90.9% set-exact accuracy against 88.0% for a model-free substring baseline and 80.9% for GPT-3.5, a margin that comes entirely from null queries, on which GPT-3.5 never abstains; on non-null queries all three stay within about a point. Because the probe's output space is exactly the fixed 49-source vocabulary, it cannot drift outside the allow-list as the prompted model does. Three design choices make it work: selecting a shallow layer, mean pooling, and class-imbalance-aware multi-label training over the long tail of sources. A 135M-parameter model lands within ~1.5 points of a 1.5B one, so the filter is cheap to output: a partial forward pass through the first few layers plus one linear head, with no API. The code is available at https://github.com/mxpoliakov/Multi-Meta-RAG.

</details>


### [96] [Can Dialects Be Steered Like Languages? Sparse Neurons and Distributed Directions in Arabic LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03936)
*Kareem Elozeiri,Mervat Abassy,Omar Kallas,Fahim Dalvi,Preslav Nakov,Kentaro Inui,Nadir Durrani*

TL;DR: 该研究提出两种无需微调即可控制阿拉伯语大模型生成方言的推理时方法，通过神经元级分析和向量引导技术，揭示了方言特征在模型内部的编码机制，并实现了对生成方言的精准调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿拉伯语自然语言处理中存在方言数据稀缺的问题，导致大模型过度生成现代标准阿拉伯语（MSA），难以准确生成方言。因此需要理解方言特征在模型内部的编码位置与方式，并探索无需微调即可控制方言生成的方法。

Method: 采用神经元级分析，识别编码方言特性的稀疏神经元群体；同时提出向量引导方法，提取方言特定的激活方向并在推理时注入，实现对输出方言的控制。

Result: 实验表明，放大或抑制特定神经元可有效引导模型生成目标方言；向量引导方法成功实现了对生成结果的方言控制，且不依赖于微调。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了阿拉伯语大模型中方言知识的内在几何结构，提出了一种基于可解释性的无微调方言控制框架，为方言生成提供了新的思路和技术手段。

Abstract: A key challenge in Arabic NLP is the scarcity of dialectal data relative to Modern Standard Arabic (MSA), causing LLMs to overproduce MSA and struggle with dialectally accurate generation. From an interpretability perspective, this raises a fundamental question: where and how are dialectal features encoded within model internals, and can these representations be leveraged to improve dialect generation without fine-tuning? This study investigates two complementary inference-time approaches that serve simultaneously as interpretability probes and control mechanisms. First, we conduct a neuron-level analysis, identifying sparse neuron populations that encode dialect-specific features and showing that amplifying or suppressing these neurons can steer model outputs toward target dialects. Second, motivated by the entanglement of dialectal features at the single-neuron level, we apply a vector-steering approach that extracts dialect-specific activation directions and injects them during inference. Together, these methods illuminate the geometry of dialectal knowledge in Arabic LLMs and offer a principled, interpretability-grounded framework for dialect control without requiring dialect-specific fine-tuning.

### [97] [The Remarkable Effectiveness of Providing AI Agents with Natural Language Tools: A Replication Study Validating NLT Performance Across 14 Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03953)
*Alexander Somma,Isabelle Plante,Fred Premji*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究独立复现并扩展了Johnson等人（2025）提出的自然语言工具（NLT）框架，验证其在14个模型、8560次试验中的有效性。NLT整体提升工具调用准确率14.9个百分点（62.3% vs 47.4%），关键错误减少93%（51 vs 755），token消耗降低25.2%。优势在无原生工具调用、推理型及小型模型中尤为显著，而前沿优化模型（如GPT-5、Gemini 2.5 Pro）收益较小甚至倒退，与强化学习优化工具使用的分析一致。在递归代理工作流中，NLT通过避免结构化失败引发的重试与协调开销，显著提升可靠性与效率。研究贡献包括：首次使用开源工具独立验证NLT；揭示模型能力调节其收益；量化其可靠性优势（93%错误减少）。结论：NLT是生产系统中可靠性的更优选择，尤其在重视稳定性而非可解析性时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑现有大型语言模型代理系统中对结构化工具调用的依赖，因其易出错且在复杂任务中导致高成本的失败重试和协调开销。旨在寻找更可靠、高效的替代方案以提升实际部署中的系统鲁棒性。

Method: 通过独立复现NLT框架，在14种模型上进行大规模实验（8560次），涵盖前沿、推理型和开源模型，评估其在工具调用准确性、错误率、token消耗及递归工作流表现上的性能，并对比原始结构化方法。

Result: NLT整体工具调用准确率提升14.9个百分点（62.3% vs 47.4%），关键错误减少93%（51 vs 755），token使用量下降25.2%。小型、无原生工具调用或推理型模型获益最大（+24.0pp 至 +43.1pp），而高度优化的前沿模型收益小或逆转。在递归代理流程中，因避免失败链式反应，其可靠性与效率优势显著放大。

Conclusion: NLT是一种比结构化工具调用更具实用价值的替代方案，尤其适用于重视可靠性与稳定性的生产环境，特别是在模型能力较弱或未专门优化工具调用的场景下。

Abstract: This study independently replicates and extends the Natural Language Tools (NLT) framework of Johnson et al.~(2025), which questions the use of structured tool calling in large language model (LLM) agentic systems. We evaluated NLT across 14 models and 8,560 trials, adding newer frontier, reasoning, and open-weight models to the original set. The results confirm the core findings and add detail. NLT improves tool-calling accuracy by 14.9 percentage points overall (62.3\% versus 47.4\% structured) and reduces critical errors by 93\% (51 versus 755 errors). The gains depend on model capability: models without native tool calling, reasoning models, and smaller models gain substantially (+24.0pp to +43.1pp), while heavily optimized frontier models (GPT-5, Gemini 2.5 Pro) show smaller or reversed advantages. This matches recent analyses of reinforcement-learning-optimized tool use (Martinez, 2025). NLT also cuts token usage by 25.2\%. The reliability and efficiency advantages compound in recursive agentic workflows, where agents chain many tool calls across sub-agents: a structured failure triggers retries, fallback routing, and coordination overhead, while NLT avoids most of that cost at the source. This work makes three contributions: (1) the first independent validation of NLT using open-source tooling, (2) evidence that model capability moderates NLT's advantages (Chen et al., 2025; Zhang et al., 2025), and (3) a measurement of NLT's reliability benefit (93\% fewer errors), its most deployment-relevant property given the known fragility of structured tool calling. NLT is a practical alternative to structured tool calling, especially for production systems that value reliability over parseability.

### [98] [NormWorlds-CF: Solver-Verified Counterfactual Normative Reasoning with Metamorphic-Relation GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03957)
*Xinqi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出NormWorlds-CF，一个用于可执行规则世界中反事实规范推理的验证环境，通过确定性求解器提供答案、证明、伪证证书、论点状态、支持集和配对世界变化标签，实现无需大语言模型裁判的监督与评估。基准测试包含分阶段SFT诊断和紧凑的配对世界任务，涵盖270个根族和1080个标准-变体对。SFT诊断显示仅基于最终答案的监督是不安全的代理：仅答案微调达到完美准确率但对伪证为零；而结合证明与伪证训练并使用目标重播的方法在所有任务上表现优异。针对结构化变化任务，引入类条件奖励MR-GRPO，给予关系家族部分得分且可见于求解器。在1.7B模型连续实验中，MR-GRPO提升未见关系准确率与关系族正确性，减少错误族错误。在Qwen3-4B三种子验证中，仅答案奖励改善答案变化字段但削弱关系族结构，稀疏奖励最好保留粗粒度关系标签，而MR-GRPO在答案变化、支持变化、状态变化及软根级元关系度量上表现最佳平衡。结果表明，经验证的反事实结构可影响微调后性能，但完整变化记录生成、不变子类型识别和分布外（OOD）迁移仍是开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型虽能给出正确的规范结论，但推理过程可能错误。需要一种可验证的反事实规范推理环境，以确保模型不仅得出正确答案，还能具备合理的推理结构，从而避免‘因错而对’的问题。传统依赖大语言模型裁判的评估方式不可靠，亟需一种可执行、可验证的基准测试框架。

Method: 提出NormWorlds-CF环境，结合确定性求解器生成最终答案、证明、伪证证书、论点状态、支持集和配对世界变化标签；设计分阶段SFT诊断任务与紧凑配对世界任务；引入类条件奖励机制MR-GRPO，用于在强化学习中对关系家族和求解器可见的变化字段给予部分奖励；采用目标重播策略增强训练效果。

Result: 答案仅微调方法在最终答案任务上达到100%准确率，但在伪证任务上得分为零；而结合证明与伪证训练并使用目标重播的方法在所有任务上均取得高准确率。在1.7B模型实验中，MR-GRPO显著提升关系族正确性和未见关系准确率，降低错误族错误。在Qwen3-4B三种子验证中，MR-GRPO在多种指标上表现最优，实现各维度间的良好平衡。

Conclusion: 经验证的反事实结构能够有效引导模型微调后的行为，超越仅关注最终答案的训练方式。然而，完整变化记录生成、不变子类型识别以及跨分布外场景的泛化能力仍待解决，是未来研究的关键方向。

Abstract: Language models can reach the right normative verdict for the wrong reason. We introduce NormWorlds-CF, a solver-verified environment for counterfactual normative reasoning in executable rule worlds. Its deterministic solver produces final answers, proof and falsification certificates, argument statuses, support sets, and paired-world change labels, enabling supervision and evaluation without LLM judges. The benchmark contains staged SFT diagnostics and a compact paired-world task with 270 root families and 1080 canonical-to-variant pairs. The SFT diagnostics show that final-answer supervision is an unsafe proxy: answer-only SFT reaches perfect accuracy on answer tasks but scores zero on falsification, while proof-plus-falsification training with targeted replay reaches strong all-task accuracy. For the structured-change task, we introduce metamorphic-relation GRPO (MR-GRPO), a class-conditioned reward for GRPO that gives partial credit for relation families and solver-visible change fields. In matched 1.7B continuation experiments, MR-GRPO improves held-out relation accuracy and relation-family correctness, and reduces wrong-family error, compared to sparse and answer-only GRPO. In Qwen3-4B three-seed validation, answer-only reward improves answer-change fields but weakens relation-family structure, sparse reward preserves coarse relation labels best, and MR-GRPO delivers the strongest balanced performance across answer-change, support-change, status-change, and soft root-level metamorphic-relation metrics. These results show that verified counterfactual structure can shape post-training beyond final answers, while exact full change-record generation, invariant subtype recognition, and out-of-distribution (OOD) transfer remain open problems.

</details>


### [99] [TRACER: Early Failure Detection for Task-Oriented Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03974)
*Erfan Nourbakhsh,Rocky Slavin,Ke Yang,Anthony Rios*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TRACER is a method for early failure detection in task-oriented dialogue systems, using trajectory signals and text representations to predict conversation failure before it becomes obvious. It performs well even with limited dialogue history (25% to 100%) and outperforms various baselines.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Most evaluation of task-oriented dialogue systems only assesses failure after the conversation has already broken down, missing opportunities for timely intervention. Early failure detection can provide practical warnings before full system failure.

Method: TRACER combines simple trajectory signals from belief-state changes with text representations of the evolving dialogue state to predict whether a conversation will fail. It is evaluated under both oracle and generated belief-state settings across different levels of dialogue visibility.

Result: TRACER detects failure signals effectively long before the end of the conversation and consistently outperforms heuristic, classical, and single-stream baselines across all tested dialogue lengths (25%, 50%, 75%, 100%).

Conclusion: Early failure detection via TRACER offers a practical and effective way to identify impending dialogue system failures, enabling timely interventions before complete breakdown.

Abstract: Task-oriented dialogue systems often fail before the final breakdown is obvious, but most evaluation only measures failure after the conversation has already gone wrong. We present TRACER, a method for early failure detection in task-oriented dialogue. TRACER predicts from a partial dialogue whether the full conversation will eventually fail by combining simple trajectory signals from belief-state changes with text representations of the evolving dialogue state. We evaluate the method in both oracle and generated belief-state settings, and test how well it works when only 25%, 50%, 75%, or 100% of the dialogue is visible. Across these settings, TRACER detects useful failure signals well before the end of the conversation and outperforms heuristic, classical, and single-stream baselines. These results suggest that early failure detection can provide a practical warning signal for dialogue systems before the interaction fully breaks down.

Conclusion: 本研究首次聚焦于孟加拉语 meme 中的证据检测任务，提出的框架与数据集为低资源语言的 meme 理解开辟新路径，推动了多模态内容分析在非主流语言中的发展。

Abstract: Memes have become influential communication tools on social media, combining viral visuals with concise messaging to convey impactful ideas. While substantial research has examined the affective dimensions of memes, key challenges such as detecting harmful content, identifying cyberbullying, and performing accurate sentiment analysis remain critical, largely due to the need for deeper contextual understanding. In this paper, we introduce MemeEvidenceDetect, a hybrid task aimed at analyzing a meme and its contextual information to identify specific sentences that explain or elucidate its meaning and humor. To support this task, we present BanglaMemeEvidence, a curated dataset of 2,917 Bengali memes, emphasizing its significance as a resource for the Bangla language. To address the gap in dynamically inferring a meme's context, we propose BengaliMemeEvidenceNet, a hybrid multimodal framework that integrates textual and visual features for comprehensive meme representation. Our experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of BengaliMemeEvidenceNet, achieving an F1 score of 0.74. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study to focus on evidence detection in Bengali memes, marking a notable step forward in the analysis of memes in low-resource languages.

### [101] [Candidate-Constrained Retrieval-Augmented Generation for LongEval-RAG: System Design and Empirical Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04008)
*Yingdong Yang,Haijian Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种候选集约束的检索增强生成系统LongEval-RAG，通过规则化分块、查询扩展、伪相关反馈、倒数排名融合、轻量级重排和引用感知证据聚合等技术，结合MiniLM句级重排，实现高效精准的生成。最强变体rule-minilm在多个指标上表现最佳，表明稳定规则分块与句级神经选择结合优于复杂语义分块。补充评估显示多指标评价的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决长文本RAG任务中检索与生成的精确性与可控性问题，确保所有证据和引用均来自组织者提供的候选集，提升结果可解释性和一致性。

Method: 采用规则分块、确定性查询扩展、伪相关反馈（PRF）、倒数排名融合（RRF）、轻量级证据重排、引用优先策略、以及可选的MiniLM句级重排，构建端到端的候选约束型RAG系统。

Result: rule-minilm变体在BERTScore、检索精度、信息点覆盖率和平均评分上均表现最优；证明规则分块与句级神经选择的组合比复杂语义分块更有效；补充评估揭示了多指标评价的必要性。

Conclusion: 在长文本RAG任务中，稳定规则分块与后期句级神经选择相结合，能显著提升生成质量与可控性；同时强调应采用多维度评估体系以全面衡量系统性能。

Abstract: We present a candidate-constrained retrieval-augmented generation system for LongEval-RAG, where each query is associated with an organizer-provided candidate set and all retrieved evidence and final citations must remain within that set. The system combines deterministic provenance tracking with passage-based retrieval, deterministic query expansion, pseudo-relevance feedback (PRF), reciprocal rank fusion (RRF), lightweight evidence reranking, citation-aware evidence aggregation, and optional MiniLM sentence reranking. We evaluate ten pipeline variants using a primary organizer evaluation and a supplementary self-generated diagnostic protocol. The primary evaluation shows that the strongest balanced variant is rule-minilm: a rule-based chunking pipeline with query expansion, PRF, RRF, reranking, citation prior, and late MiniLM sentence selection. This variant obtains the highest BERTScore, retrieval precision, nugget coverage, and average grade among our submissions. The result suggests that the main gain does not come from more complex semantic or topic-shift chunking, but from pairing stable rule-based evidence units with sentence-level neural selection before generation. The supplementary LLM-judge evaluation remains useful for early diagnosis and additional analysis, but it emphasizes different systems than the primary gold-answer and nugget-based evaluation, highlighting the need for multi-metric RAG evaluation.

### [102] [Separating Representation from Reconstruction Enables Scalable Text Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04011)
*Megi Dervishi,Mathurin Videau,Yann LeCun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在解码器快速扩展的背景下，编码器（如BERT）仍保持不变的问题。通过冻结主干评估和探针分析发现，尽管困惑度提升，BERT编码器的表示能力反而变得越来越难以被探针利用，根源在于其扁平结构将表示学习与词元重建损失耦合。为此，作者提出CrossBERT，一种两部分架构，将高质量表示学习与词元重建解耦，并引入互补掩码策略，支持高掩码率（≥50%）和全词元梯度计算，从而实现1.5到2倍的吞吐量提升和2倍的样本效率提升。CrossBERT表现出单调扩展性，在MTEB(eng, v2)和冻结GLUE基准测试中均取得优异性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前解码器快速发展，但编码器（如BERT）设计长期未变，其扁平结构导致表示学习与词元重建任务耦合，限制了表示质量的进一步提升。需要一种新的编码器架构来解耦表示学习与重建任务，以提升模型性能和效率。

Method: 提出CrossBERT，采用两部分架构：第一部分专注于高质量表示学习，第二部分负责词元重建；引入互补掩码策略，支持高掩码率（≥50%）和对所有词元的梯度计算，实现高效训练与推理。

Result: CrossBERT在高掩码率下实现1.5至2倍的吞吐量提升，样本效率提升2倍；在MTEB(eng, v2)和冻结GLUE基准上表现优于现有方法，展现出单调扩展性与优越性能。

Conclusion: CrossBERT通过解耦表示学习与词元重建任务，克服了BERT式编码器的固有局限，显著提升了编码器的表达能力和训练效率，为大规模语言模型的编码器设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: While decoders have rapidly scaled, encoders have remained largely unchanged since BERT. We revisit this disparity by frozen backbone evaluation via probing. Under this lens, the representations of BERT encoders become increasingly $\textit{unexploitable}$ by frozen probes, despite improved perplexity. The misalignment originates in BERT's flat design, which couples representation learning to the token reconstruction loss. We propose $\textbf{CrossBERT}$, a two-part architecture that separates the learning of high-quality encoded representations from the rigid grounding of token reconstruction. This design further enables high masking ratios ($\ge 50\%$) and gradient collection over all tokens via a $\textit{Complementary Masking Strategy}$, respectively increasing throughput by $1.5$ to $2\times$ and sample efficiency by $2\times$. Overall, CrossBERT demonstrates monotonic scaling and superior performance on MTEB(eng, v2) and frozen GLUE benchmarks.

### [103] [CrossHallu: Do Hallucination Signals Generalize Across Languages and Domains in Large Language Model's Internals?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04029)
*Aisha Alansari,Malak Alkhorasani,Hamzah Luqman*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CrossHallu 是首个系统评估大语言模型内部表示在跨语言和跨领域场景下幻觉检测泛化能力的研究。通过在阿拉伯语与英语之间、不同数据集间的对比实验，发现大多数模型的内部幻觉信号具有跨语言和跨域迁移能力，但性能受特征空间中类别可分性和语言对齐度的影响，且阿拉伯语内部的跨域迁移效果依赖于具体训练与测试数据。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测方法主要集中在英文语境，缺乏对多语言和跨领域泛化能力的系统评估，因此亟需研究内部表示在不同语言和领域间是否有效迁移。

Method: 采用六种大语言模型，在生成式问答任务上进行阿拉伯语与英语之间的交叉评估，涵盖单语、跨语言、跨域及联合跨语言与跨域转移等多种设置，并使用 TruthfulQA 及其阿拉伯语翻译版、HalluScore 作为评测基准。

Result: 大多数模型的内部幻觉信号可在跨语言和跨域场景下成功迁移；跨语言性能受特征空间中类别分离程度和语言对齐性影响显著；跨域性能在阿拉伯语中因数据集差异而表现不一。

Conclusion: 内部表示中的幻觉信号具备一定的跨语言和跨域泛化能力，但其有效性取决于语言对齐与数据分布匹配程度，提示未来工作应关注特征空间的跨语言一致性与领域适应性设计。

Abstract: Recent hallucination detection techniques in large language models (LLMs) focus on directly extracting features from a model's internal representations and training a classifier on these features to detect hallucinations, demonstrating promising results. Notwithstanding this advancement, most internal-state hallucination detection techniques have been explored predominantly in English, raising the question of whether such internal signals generalize across different languages and domains. To address this gap, we present CrossHallu, the first study to evaluate the cross-lingual and cross-domain generalization of hallucination detection using internal representations from six LLMs on the generative question-answering task. We conduct a systematic Arabic <-> English evaluation using TruthfulQA, an Arabic translated version of TruthfulQA, and HalluScore. This evaluation encompasses monolingual training and testing, cross-lingual transfer, cross-domain transfer, and combined cross-lingual and cross-domain transfer. The results reveal that internal-state hallucination signals in LLMs transfer across languages and domains for most models, with cross-lingual performance highly dependent on both class separability and language alignment in the feature space, whereas cross-domain transfer within Arabic varies depending on the training and testing datasets used for the hallucination detector. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/aishaalansari57/CrossHal.

### [104] [Telescope: Improving Zero Shot Detection of LLM Generated Content By Measuring Token Repetition Probability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04061)
*Christopher Nassif,Josh F. Cooper*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为Telescope Perplexity的新指标，用于检测大语言模型（LLM）生成文本与人类写作的区别。研究发现，LLM在训练早期便形成对词元重复的强烈规避倾向，这种倾向作为‘遗留启发法’在生成文本中持续存在，可作为区分依据。实验表明，Telescope Perplexity在零样本场景下表现优异，且在多个数据集和扰动条件下均达到或超过现有水平，同时效率更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前区分大语言模型生成文本与人类写作面临挑战，尽管LLM被训练得像人类，但其训练过程留下了可探测的痕迹——对词元重复的异常规避。这一现象可能成为识别生成文本的有效线索。

Method: 提出Telescope Perplexity指标，通过评估上下文条件下词元重复的概率分布来捕捉模型对重复的敏感性。利用该指标进行零样本检测，并在多种数据集和扰动设置下验证其有效性。

Result: Telescope Perplexity在多个基准数据集上表现出色，实现高精度的零样本检测，优于或媲美现有方法，且计算效率更高。

Conclusion: LLM生成文本中存在由训练过程引发的固有模式——对词元重复的过度规避，这可通过Telescope Perplexity有效捕捉，为检测生成内容提供高效、鲁棒的新途径。

Abstract: Distinguishing Large Language Model (LLM) generated text from human writing is a critical and difficult challenge. While LLMs are trained to write like humans, we hypothesize that this training leaves an indelible mark. LLMs develop a particularly strong aversion to token repetition very early in training. This bias persists as a ''Vestigial Heuristic'' (a developmental artifact) that is activated in LLM-generated text, separating LLM from human writing. To probe this phenomenon, we introduce Telescope Perplexity, a metric that evaluates the token repetition of the model, $P(s_i | s_{1:i})$ . Our empirical investigation reveals that the Telescope Perplexity signature emerges early in pre-training, and Telescope Perplexity empirically enables highly effective zero-shot LLM detection. We show state-of-the-art or competitive performance across diverse datasets (including modern evaluation sets we introduce), reference models, and perturbation schemes with greater efficiency than other methods.

To address this problem, we propose a speaker-disentangled syllabic tokenizer that regresses speaker-perturbed student representations toward clean teacher targets within fixed-length chunks. Experimental results demonstrate that our proposed method achieves state-of-the-art performance in syllable boundary detection and syllabic segment clustering. Moreover, a speech language model trained on our syllabic tokens achieves a 7% relative improvement in syntactic and semantic understanding over the phone-level SpiRit-LM.

### [106] [Beyond Multilingual Averages: MTEB-PT, a Benchmark for Portuguese Sentence Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04071)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 葡萄牙语在文本嵌入评估中仍被严重低估，尽管其是全球使用最广泛的语言之一。现有模型选择多基于英语或多语言指标，但其在葡萄牙语上的实际效果尚不明确。因此，亟需一个专门针对葡萄牙语的评估基准以准确衡量嵌入模型的表现，并探索语言特定微调的有效性。

Method: 构建MTEB-PT基准，从MMTEB中选取14个数据集，涵盖多种任务类型；采用统一评估协议对17个嵌入模型进行测试；通过葡萄牙语对比监督和Matryoshka表示学习（MRL）对三类主干模型进行微调；分析不同任务下模型表现差异及微调效果。

Result: 葡萄牙语表现具有强任务依赖性，多语言排名不能有效预测葡萄牙语表现；无模型在所有任务中领先；长上下文能力对长输入任务（如检索、重排序）有显著优势；语言特定微调可提升性能，尤其在与训练数据匹配的任务上；微调后的模型在STS任务上增益最大，同时提升检索性能并在维度截断下保持竞争力。

Conclusion: MTEB-PT为葡萄牙语嵌入模型提供了可靠的评估基准，揭示了模型表现的多样性与任务相关性。语言特定微调仍具价值，尤其是在任务与训练数据一致时。本研究推动了葡萄牙语自然语言处理的发展，并为未来模型开发与评估提供重要参考。

Abstract: Portuguese remains underrepresented in text embedding evaluation, despite being one of the most widely spoken languages in the world. As a result, embedding models are often selected based on English or multilingual metrics, while their effectiveness in Portuguese remains unclear. We present MTEB-PT, a Portuguese benchmark constructed from a subset of MMTEB, comprising 14 existing datasets across Semantic Textual Similarity (STS), classification, retrieval, and reranking. We use this benchmark to evaluate 17 open- and closed-source embedding models under a unified protocol. Our results show that Portuguese performance is strongly task-dependent: multilingual rankings do not reliably predict Portuguese-specific performance across task families, no single model dominates all settings, and models with stronger long-context capacity are particularly advantageous on longer-input tasks such as retrieval and reranking. The benchmark also shows that language-specific fine-tuning still improves model performance in Portuguese, especially on task types that match the adaptation data most closely. To examine this effect, we fine-tune three representative backbone models with Portuguese contrastive supervision and Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL). These benchmark-informed baselines yield their strongest gains on STS, consistent with the predominantly symmetric supervision used during training, while also improving retrieval and remaining competitive under dimensional truncation. We release the MTEB-PT benchmark, the fine-tuned models, and the training and evaluation code.

### [107] [Semantic Integration and Lexical Expectation Shape N400 and P600 Dynamics During Naturalistic Reading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04107)
*Kun Sun,Rong Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究利用DERCo数据集，探讨了语境语义相关性是否在自然阅读中解释神经反应的变异，超越词汇预期。通过回归和广义加性混合模型分析发现，语境语义相关性在N400和P600窗口均表现出显著效应，尤其在P600窗口更强，且其解释力超越了词汇控制和词意外度（surprisal）。结果表明，自然阅读同时依赖词汇预期与局部语义整合，语境语义相关性为话语语义契合与脑电活动提供了可解释的计算桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语境语义相关性是否能解释人类阅读时的神经反应，超越传统词意外度模型，以更全面理解语言理解中的认知机制。

Method: 基于DERCo数据集，使用22名参与者和32个EEG通道，采用回归型ERP分析和广义加性混合模型，比较语境语义相关性和GPT-based词意外度对脑电活动（N400和P600窗口）的预测能力，控制词汇变量和重复观测。

Result: 两个预测因子均与脑电反应显著相关，但表现不同：词意外度反映预期相关变化，而语境语义相关性在N400和P600窗口均有强效应，尤其在P600窗口突出；模型比较显示其提供额外解释力，超越词汇控制和词意外度。

Conclusion: 自然阅读不仅依赖词汇预期，也依赖局部语义整合；语境语义相关性是连接话语语义契合与脑电动态的有力、可解释的计算指标。

Abstract: Word surprisal is a well-established computational predictor of human neural responses during language comprehension, but it remains less clear whether local semantic fit explains neural response variation beyond lexical expectation during naturalistic reading. Using the Dublin EEG-based Reading Experiment Corpus (DERCo), this study examined whether contextual semantic relevance predicts word-locked EEG activity in the N400 and P600 windows. Contextual semantic relevance was computed as an attention-aware measure of how strongly a target word is semantically connected to its recent discourse context, and it was compared with GPT-based word surprisal. Across 22 participants and 32 EEG channels, we tested both predictors using regression-based ERP analyses and generalized additive mixed models while controlling for lexical variables and repeated observations. Both predictors were reliably associated with EEG responses, but they showed partly different temporal and scalp-level patterns. Surprisal captured expectancy-related variation, whereas contextual semantic relevance showed robust effects across N400- and P600-window mean voltages, with particularly strong explanatory support in the P600 window. Model comparisons indicated that contextual semantic relevance contributed explanatory value beyond lexical controls and surprisal. These findings suggest that naturalistic reading depends on both lexical expectation and local semantic integration, and that contextual semantic relevance offers an interpretable computational link between discourse semantic fit and ERP dynamics.

### [108] [Detecting Hallucinations in Retrieval-Augmented Generation through Grounding-Aware Sensitivity by Perturbation (GASP)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04223)
*Mohamed Aly Bouke*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GASP 是一种新的 span-level 检测方法，通过测量答案句子对检索证据的依赖程度（即“基础敏感性”）来识别幻觉。它在固定答案的前提下，通过移除不同上下文片段并观察其似然度变化和 Jensen-Shannon 散度，判断句子是否真正基于证据生成。该方法在 RAGTruth 基准上表现优异，响应级 AUC 达 0.73，span 级 AUC 达 0.67，显著优于现有方法。其信号可迁移至 TofuEval，但在短答案问答任务中无效，表明其更适合基于检索上下文生成的输出。此外，无需训练的阈值策略即可达到与有监督分类器相当的效果，具有实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RAG 检测方法仅提供整体得分，无法定位具体幻觉句子及其原因；需要一种能精确识别幻觉位置并解释其成因的 span-level 检测机制。

Method: 提出 GASP：固定答案，分别在完整上下文、无上下文及逐个移除检索块的条件下重新评分，计算似然度下降和 JSD，利用这些变化衡量句子对证据的依赖性（即基础敏感性）。将解码视为随机非线性迭代函数系统（RNIFS）以解释其理论依据。

Result: 在 RAGTruth 基准上，响应级 AUC 达 0.73，span 级 AUC 达 0.67，显著优于困惑度、长度、全上下文 NLI 和自一致性等基线。唯一在 span 级别接近的基线是需额外模型的块级蕴含验证器，而无需训练的阈值策略表现良好，成为默认检测器。信号可在 TofuEval 中迁移，但在 RAGBench 的短答案任务中失效，说明其适用于依赖检索内容的生成输出。

Conclusion: GASP 成功实现了高精度的 span-level 幻觉检测，具备无需训练的实用阈值策略，且对基于检索上下文生成的内容具有强适应性，为 RAG 输出的可信性评估提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) reduces but does not eliminate hallucination, and existing detectors return a single answer-level score that does not indicate which sentence is unsupported, or why. To close this gap, we introduce Grounding-Aware Sensitivity by Perturbation (GASP), a span-level detector that scores each answer sentence by how strongly its likelihood depends on the retrieved evidence, a quantity we term grounding sensitivity. GASP holds the answer fixed and re-scores it under the full context, under no context, and with each chunk removed, then measures the log-likelihood drops and Jensen-Shannon divergences (JSD). The likelihood of a grounded sentence collapses once its supporting passage is removed, whereas a hallucinated sentence is almost unaffected, a contrast we interpret by casting decoding as a random nonlinear iterated function system (RNIFS). We evaluate GASP on three benchmarks (RAGTruth, TofuEval, RAGBench) with three instruction-tuned scorers from two model families (Qwen2.5-0.5B, Qwen2.5-1.5B, and SmolLM2-1.7B) under a leakage-clean protocol. On RAGTruth it reaches a response-level area under the ROC curve (AUC) of about 0.73 and a span-level AUC of about 0.67, improving significantly over perplexity and by clear margins over length, whole-context natural language inference (NLI), and self-consistency baselines. The only baseline competitive at the span level is a well-configured chunk-level entailment verifier, which requires a separate model, whereas a training-free threshold on the grounding features matches the trained classifier without labeled data and serves as the default detector. Beyond RAGTruth, the signal transfers to TofuEval but not to short-answer question answering in RAGBench, showing GASP is best suited to outputs constructed from the retrieved context rather than answers recoverable from parametric knowledge.

### [109] [Spinning Straw into Gold: Relabeling LLM Agent Trajectories in Hindsight for Successful Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04235)
*Zichao Li,Gang Wu,Zichao Wang,Ruiyi Zhang,Wanrong Zhu,Ryan A. Rossi,Vlad I Morariu,Jihyung Kil*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为事后监督学习（HSL）的新方法，利用智能体轨迹中意外但成功的自然语言目标作为监督信号，通过辅助大模型重标注轨迹中的达成目标，并用于后续微调。该方法在长时程、部分可观测任务中表现优异，尤其在目标空间多样性的任务上提升显著，且样本效率高，仅用1/4的标注数据即超越全量数据训练的基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练方法缺乏对智能体轨迹中隐含成功目标的利用，而这些目标可作为有效的监督信号，有助于缓解长时程任务中监督数据稀缺的问题。

Method: 提出HSL框架，通过一个辅助大模型分析完成的轨迹，提取并重标注其中实际达成的自然语言目标；结合无关动作掩码和样本重加权技术以减少标签偏差，再将重标注的轨迹-目标对用于模型微调。

Result: HSL在多种任务上均优于标准SFT和DPO方法，特别是在长时程、目标多样性高的任务上提升明显；在ALFWorld数据集上仅使用1/4真实演示数据即可超过全量数据训练的基线，证明其高效性。

Conclusion: HSL是一种灵活且高效的后训练方法，能够有效挖掘智能体轨迹中蕴含的成功目标信息，显著提升模型在复杂、长期任务中的表现，同时大幅降低对人工标注数据的依赖。

Abstract: Large language model agents operate in partially observable, long-horizon settings where obtaining supervision remains a major bottleneck. We address this by utilizing a source of supervision overlooked in existing post-training methods: unintended yet successful goals embedded within agent rollouts. Specifically, we introduce Hindsight Supervised Learning (HSL), where an auxiliary LLM reviews each completed trajectory and relabels it with all of the natural-language goals the agent actually achieved. HSL then pairs the trajectory with its relabeled goals and uses these pairs for additional fine-tuning. To mitigate suboptimality in the relabeled data, we propose two learning techniques for HSL, irrelevant-action masking and sample reweighting. Our experiments show that HSL is flexible and compatible with existing post-training pipelines. It improves both SFT and DPO, with larger gains on long-horizon tasks with more diverse goal spaces. Moreover, HSL is sample-efficient: on ALFWorld, it surpasses baselines trained on the full dataset while using only one quarter of the ground-truth demonstrations.

### [110] [Risk-Constrained Freshness-Aware Semantic Caching for Open-Web Retrieval-Augmented LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04281)
*Muhammad Mansoor,Tahir Ahmad,Yeo-Chan Yoon*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FreshCache 是一种三层次语义缓存系统，将缓存重用建模为风险约束的时序推理问题。它通过拟合的指数衰减模型结合学习的 MLP 来估计缓存结果过时的概率，并在概率低于各层级误差预算（答案: 0.10, URL 列表: 0.20, 页面内容: 0.35）时批准缓存命中，实现渐进式退化而非二元选择。引入 FreshCache-Bench 基准测试集（8,072 个基础查询，扩展至 31,201 个），在 24 小时评估窗口下，FreshCache_MLP 实现 97% 搜索 API 节省，仅 0.1% 哈希基过时错误；LLM 判定显示仅 34.3% 内容变化影响答案正确性，真实影响答案的过时错误约为 0.034%。规则版 FreshCache 实现 98% 节省，3.3% 过时错误，优于 SemanticTTL、vCache、SCALM。消融实验表明，时间风险门控使过时错误降低 11.6 点，学习的 MLP 再降低 3.2 点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语义缓存方法未充分建模开放网络证据的时间动态新鲜度，导致缓存命中可能带来过时结果，影响 RAG 系统的准确性和可靠性。需要一种能评估缓存项随时间变化的可信度并动态控制重用风险的方法。

Method: 提出三层次语义缓存 FreshCache，将缓存重用视为风险约束的时序推理问题。使用拟合的指数衰减模型结合学习的 MLP 估计缓存结果过时概率，依据不同层级设定误差预算（答案: 0.10, URL 列表: 0.20, 内容: 0.35），仅当过时概率低于阈值时才允许缓存命中。同时构建 FreshCache-Bench 基准，包含真实网页快照对比数据与同义句生成扩增。

Result: 在 24 小时评估窗口中，FreshCache_MLP 达到 97% 搜索 API 节省，哈希基过时错误仅 0.1%，真实影响答案的过时错误约为 0.034%；规则版 FreshCache 实现 98% 节省，3.3% 过时错误，显著优于 SemanticTTL（14.9%）、vCache（7.2%）、SCALM（5.2%）。消融实验验证了时间风险门控和 MLP 的有效性，分别降低过时错误 11.6 和 3.2 个百分点。

Conclusion: FreshCache 通过引入时间敏感的风险控制机制，实现了对语义缓存中过时风险的精细化管理，在大幅节省检索成本的同时保持高准确性。其设计支持缓存结果的渐进式退化，避免了传统方法中的二元决策缺陷，是 RAG 系统中高效、可靠缓存策略的重要进展。

Abstract: Semantic caching reduces the latency and cost of retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) by serving cached answers to semantically similar queries, but most existing methods do not model the time-varying freshness of open-web evidence. We present FreshCache, a three-tier semantic cache that treats cache reuse as a risk-constrained temporal inference problem: before approving a cache hit, FreshCache estimates the probability that the cached result is stale using a fitted exponential decay model enhanced by a learned MLP, and approves reuse only when that probability falls below a per-tier error budget across answers (epsilon = 0.10), URL lists (epsilon = 0.20), and page content (epsilon = 0.35). This allows the system to degrade gracefully as entries age rather than forcing a binary choice between a stale hit and a full pipeline execution. We introduce FreshCache-Bench, a benchmark of 8,072 base queries across five freshness classes with ground truth staleness labels drawn from real web snapshots at 1, 12, 24 hours, and 7 days after a baseline crawl, expanded to 31,201 queries via paraphrase generation. At the 24-hour evaluation window, FreshCache_MLP achieves 97% search API savings at 0.1% hash-based stale error, and an LLM-judge evaluation on 396 confirmed change pairs shows that only 34.3% of detected content changes actually affect answer correctness, placing true answer-affecting stale error at approximately 0.034%. The rule-based FreshCache achieves 98% search savings at 3.3% stale error under a temporal holdout calibration, outperforming SemanticTTL (14.9% stale, 72% saved), vCache (7.2% stale, 47% saved), and SCALM (5.2% stale, 96% saved). Ablations show the temporal risk gate accounts for an 11.6 point reduction in stale error over similarity-only reuse, and the learned MLP reduces stale error a further 3.2 points over the rule-based model.

### [111] [CausalGame: Benchmarking Causal Thinking of LLM Agents in Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04293)
*Zhenhao Chen,Yongqiang Chen,Chenxi Liu,Junchi Yu,Xiangchen Song,Zijian Li,Jialin Li,Philip Torr,Bo Han,Kun Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CausalGame 是一个评估大语言模型（LLM）在科学发现中因果思维能力的基准测试，通过互动游戏形式考察模型设计实验、收集数据并给出解释报告的能力。该基准包含14种模拟真实科学研究挑战的场景，涵盖选择偏差、测量误差和隐藏混杂因素。在30个LLM代理中，没有一个表现出可靠的因果推理能力，最佳模型仅达到68.0%的生存率，远低于分析最优解的78-85%，且仅有5-7%的会话获得因果推理评分认可。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI科学家基准未充分涵盖真实科学发现中的关键挑战，如选择偏差、测量误差和隐藏混杂因素，因此需要一个能系统评估因果思维能力的新基准。

Method: 设计名为CausalGame的交互式游戏基准，包含14种包含现实挑战的科学场景，要求LLM主动设计实验、收集数据并生成解释报告，以评估其因果推理能力。

Conclusion: CausalGame为评估AI科学家代理的因果思维能力提供了一个可扩展、受控的测试平台，揭示了当前LLM在因果推理方面的重大局限性。

Abstract: Building AI Scientist agents with Large Language Models (LLMs) has recently attracted growing attention. Since scientific discovery fundamentally relies on uncovering causal relationships from observations, the capability of causal thinking, i.e., distinguishing causation from correlation and recognizing hidden biases, is essential to LLM agents. Although a number of benchmarks exist for AI Scientists, none explicitly incorporate challenges from selection bias, measurement error, and hidden confounders that widely exist in real-world scientific discovery. To this end, we present CausalGame, a benchmark that evaluates the causal thinking capabilities of LLM agents through interactive games. CausalGame asks LLM agents to actively design experimental protocols, collect observation data, and derive a final solution with an explanation report. To emulate realistic scientific discovery challenges, we design 14 scenarios that incorporate selection bias, measurement error, and hidden confounders. Across 30 LLM agents, none demonstrates reliable causal thinking: the best model reaches only 68.0% survival against analytical optima of 78-85%, and merely 5-7% of sessions receive credits on the causal-reasoning rubrics. CausalGame provides a scalable and controlled testbed for evaluating the causal thinking of AI Scientist agents.

### [112] [Legible-by-Construction: Attention and End-to-End Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04319)
*Mark Oskin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文将前馈层中可解释的模糊集合操作思想扩展到注意力机制，通过在注意力头的值上应用sigmoid函数，使每个值通道成为可读的特征检测器，无需增加参数。进一步提出布尔变体，将值重构为显式的词内交集和可否定的差集操作。输出投影保持自由，不绑定词汇表，从而实现选择性检测。在5种专用注意力设计中，44%至62%的值通道变为清晰、上下文敏感的检测器，且其可读性随网络深度提升而非仅在标点处显现。语言模型性能与标准基线相当，并成功构建了一个端到端可解释的语言模型，其前馈单元始终为命名的集合与量化操作，可直接解读生成结果的组成逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升Transformer模型的可解释性，特别是注意力机制部分，使其内部操作具有明确的语义含义，同时保持语言模型性能不变。

Method: 在注意力头的值上使用sigmoid函数，将值通道转化为可读的特征检测器；提出布尔变体，重构值为显式集合运算（交集与差集）；保持输出投影自由，不限制写入内容，以实现选择性检测。

Result: 在125M参数规模下，44%-62%的值通道成为清晰、上下文敏感的检测器，可读性随深度增强；语言模型质量与基准持平；成功训练出一个端到端可解释的模型，生成结果可被逐层解读为命名逻辑操作的组合。

Conclusion: 通过将注意力机制设计为基于集合运算的可读检测器，并结合已有的可解释前馈层，实现了端到端可解释的语言模型，既保持了性能，又具备清晰的语义结构，为理解神经语言模型提供了新范式。

Abstract: A companion paper showed that a transformer's feed-forward layer can be rebuilt from explicit fuzzy set operations - intersection, set-difference, and a self-forgetting sequence quantifier - so its hidden units read as named logical operators at no cost to language-model quality. That left the other half of the transformer opaque. Here we carry the same idea into attention and join the two into one model. The mechanism is minimal: a head's value is passed through a sigmoid, so each value channel becomes a readable detector of whether a feature holds at a token. This adds no parameters and leaves the standard head otherwise untouched. A Boolean variant goes further, restructuring the value into an explicit within-token intersection and negation-capable set-difference. In both designs the output projection is left free, not tied to the vocabulary, which is the load-bearing decision: bounding what a head detects while leaving what it writes unconstrained yields selective detectors, whereas constraining the write does not. A bounded value is shaped into a readable detector by two selectivity pressures - one for sparse firing, one for decisive firing at the rails - and which a design wants is not universal. Across five specialized-attention designs at 125M parameters, 44 to 62 percent of value channels become crisp, contextually selective detectors, and their legibility rises with depth rather than crystallizing only on punctuation. Language-model quality is at parity with a conventional baseline. Finally, we couple the Boolean attention to the legible feed-forward layer and train an end-to-end legible-by-construction language model at benchmark parity: its feed-forward units are named set and quantifier operations throughout, and we can take a token it generates and read the named units that compose to produce it.

</details>


### [113] [WPG-MoE: Weak-Prior-Guided Dense Mixture-of-Experts for User-Level Social Media Depression Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04350)
*Xian Li,Yuanhe Tian,Yang Yang,Guoqing Wang,Yan Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出WPG-MoE框架，利用弱先验引导的密集专家混合模型，通过共享大语言模型骨干网络，基于用户级弱语义先验软路由至匹配不同证据布局的专家，解决单一检测器在异构用户表达上的局限性，实现更精准、可解释的抑郁早期筛查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖单一检测器进行最终决策，忽略了用户在筛查后表达抑郁风险的异质性，导致局部证据被稀释，尤其对非自我披露用户易产生误判。

Method: 提出WPG-MoE框架，基于共享大语言模型骨干网络，利用弱语义先验对用户进行软路由，使不同用户被分配至适合其证据结构的专家；训练阶段采用学习使用特权信息（LUPI）机制，利用大模型提取的结构化证据指导路由，推理时仅保留PHQ-9模板和可部署骨干网络。

Result: 在中英文数据集上的实验表明，WPG-MoE优于强基线模型，具备可解释的路由行为，提升了抑郁筛查的准确性和适应性。

Conclusion: WPG-MoE通过弱先验引导的专家路由机制，有效应对用户表达异质性问题，显著提升在线社交媒介中抑郁早期筛查的性能与可解释性。

Abstract: Online social media posts provide scalable signals for early depression screening, and recent studies mainly improve pre-classification evidence through risk-post selection, symptom grounding, and clinically informed feature construction. However, these screening-stage designs often leave final decisions to a single detector, overlooking how users heterogeneously express depressive risk after screening. A monolithic classifier must average across heterogeneous users, which may dilute localized evidence and cause misclassification, especially for non-self-disclosing users. To address this issue, we propose WPG-MoE, a weak-prior-guided dense mixture-of-experts framework built on a shared large language model (LLM) backbone. WPG-MoE derives user-level weak semantic priors to softly route users to experts matched to different evidence layouts. We formulate this process as learning using privileged information (LUPI): rich LLM-extracted structured evidence guides training-time routing, while inference retains only Patient Health Questionnaire-9 (PHQ-9) template screening and the deployable backbone. Experiments on Chinese and English datasets show that WPG-MoE outperforms strong baselines with interpretable routing behavior.

### [114] [Auditing the Audit: Five Failure Modes in Benchmark-Validity Audits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02586)
*Yanhang Li,Zhichao Fan,Zexin Zhuang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，基于扰动的构造有效性审计在AI评估中虽常见，但其结论可能因不可见的实现细节而被无声伪造。作者通过一个包含两个模型和五个基准测试的案例研究，揭示了五类管道失败，并提出六点尽职调查门禁作为保障级证据的披露与保留协议，强调该方法补充而非替代传统验证证据，不用于判定基准有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前治理框架要求提供可文档化的评估证据，其中扰动基构造有效性审计是常见形式。然而，这些审计结果可能受隐蔽的实现细节影响，导致结论不可靠，因此需要更严格的审查机制。

Method: 通过自审计方式，在安全基准测试和开源权重指令微调模型上演示五类管道失败；提出六点尽职调查门禁作为评估证据的披露与保留协议。

Result: 所有测试单元均落入非确认性类别，无一达到确认性标准，表明现有审计方法存在显著脆弱性。

Conclusion: 应将六点尽职调查门禁作为补充性协议，用于提升评估证据的可信度，而非取代传统构造有效性验证或得出基准有效性结论。

Abstract: Governance frameworks ask AI providers and auditors for documented evaluation evidence, and perturbation-based construct-validity audits are a common form of that evidence. We argue the audits are themselves fragile: their conclusions can be silently manufactured by implementation details that readers cannot see in the reported numbers. We name five classes of pipeline failure and demonstrate each in a self-audit over safety benchmarks and open-weight instruction-tuned models. Under a unified six-point due-diligence gate, every cell lands in a non-confirmatory bucket, and no cell reaches confirmatory. The evidence here is a single two-model, five-benchmark case study, and F1--F5 is an illustrative, deliberately non-exhaustive starting taxonomy -- not a comprehensive partition of audit failures. We position the gate as a withholding and disclosure protocol for assurance-grade evidence, supplementary to (not a replacement for) classical construct-validity evidence, and not as a route to benchmark-validity verdicts.

</details>


### [115] [Evaluating Time Series Foundation Models for Electricity Price Forecasting: Contamination Risk, Distributional Shifts, and Covariate Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02623)
*Zhenghua Pan,Ahmed Aziz Ezzat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个双数据集基准框架用于电力价格预测（EPF），以减少数据污染风险并实现对时间序列基础模型（TSFMs）的公平评估。研究发现TSFMs在零样本预测中表现优异，尤其在点预测和概率预测方面竞争力强，但其性能高度依赖协变量支持，且并未始终超越专门针对EPF设计的方法。有趣的是，简单集成TSFMs与领域特定方法表现出显著潜力，表明两者捕捉了互补的预测信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间序列基础模型（TSFMs）在具有协变量驱动、非平稳特性的电力价格预测（EPF）场景下的泛化能力，解决现有评估中存在的数据污染问题，并比较其与领域特定方法的性能差异。

Method: 提出一个双数据集基准框架，用于电力价格预测任务；系统评估TSFMs在点预测、概率预测、尾部行为、价格尖峰等方面的性能，并与领域特定方法进行对比分析。

Result: TSFMs在多数指标上表现良好，具备较强的零样本预测能力，但在依赖协变量时性能更优；其表现虽常优于通用基线，但未一致超越专为EPF设计的方法；简单集成策略展现出巨大潜力，说明两类方法具有互补性。

Conclusion: 时间序列基础模型在电力价格预测中表现强劲，但其优势依赖于协变量输入；结合领域特定方法的集成策略可能成为未来提升预测性能的有效路径。

Abstract: Time series foundation models (TSFMs) have shown strong zero-shot forecasting performance, but their generalization in covariate-driven, non-stationary settings is underexplored. Electricity price forecasting (EPF) presents a challenging testbed due to complex temporal dependencies, distributional shifts, and strong reliance on structural and contextual information. We propose a two-dataset-benchmarking framework for EPF to mitigate contamination risk and enable fair evaluation of TSFMs. We examine key aspects of EPF including point and probabilistic forecasting performance, tail behavior, price spikes, and comparisons against domain-specific methods. We find that TSFMs are highly competitive and often outperform general-purpose baselines. Yet, their performance depends critically on covariate support, and they do not consistently surpass domain-specific methods tailored to EPF. Interestingly, simple ensembles of TSFMs and domain-specific methods appear to have significant potential, suggesting that the two approaches capture complementary predictive information.

### [116] [QuantFlow: A Federated Mamba-Based Post-Transformer Foundation Model for Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02632)
*Shah Nawaz Haider,Steve Austin,Arnab Barua,Sarowar Morshed Shawon,Hadaate Ullah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QuantFlow 是一种结合了反向序列嵌入、双向 Mamba 状态空间解码器、分位数回归和联邦学习的概率时间序列预测框架，适用于长时序、高维且隐私敏感的数据。通过在完整观测窗口内对每个变量进行双向处理并投影到五个条件分位数，同时利用 TSMixup 保持序列结构的同时扩展时间多样性，该方法在加密货币、交通、电力、变压器温度、流感和天气数据上表现出色，在 ETTm1 和 Weather 数据集上分别达到 0.2834 和 0.2218 的均方误差，并在 20 客户端非独立同分布设置下仅需三轮通信即可保持有效精度，无需集中原始数据。结果表明，选择性状态空间建模是可扩展、不确定性感知和隐私友好的时间序列预测的有前景基础，但对不规则流行病学信号和长周期泛化仍存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列预测模型依赖集中式数据和 Transformer 注意力机制，难以应对长时序、高维及隐私敏感场景，亟需更高效、安全且具备不确定性表达能力的新方法。

Method: QuantFlow 采用反向序列嵌入、双向 Mamba 状态空间解码器、分位数回归与联邦学习相结合的方式，对每个变量在完整观测窗口内进行双向处理，输出五种条件分位数；引入 TSMixup 通过狄利克雷加权插值增强时间多样性，同时保留序列结构。

Result: 在多个真实世界数据集（包括加密货币、交通、电力、变压器温度、流感和天气）上验证，QuantFlow 在 ETTm1 上取得 0.2834 的均方误差，在 Weather 上为 0.2218；在 20 客户端非独立同分布环境下，仅经过三轮通信即保持有用精度，无需集中原始数据。

Conclusion: 选择性状态空间建模为可扩展、不确定性感知和隐私保护的时间序列预测提供了有前景的方向，但在不规则流行病学信号和长期预测任务中仍存在挑战。

Abstract: Time-series forecasting supports decisions in finance, en-ergy, transportation, public health, and industrial monitoring. Recent foundation models improve transfer across forecast-ing tasks, but many depend on centralized data and Trans-former attention, which restricts their use for long, high-di-mensional, and privacy-sensitive signals. This paper presents QuantFlow, a probabilistic forecasting framework that com-bines inverted sequence embedding, bidirectional Mamba state-space decoders, quantile regression, and federated learning. Each variable is embedded over the complete ob-servation window, processed in forward and reverse direc-tions, and projected to five conditional quantiles. TSMixup expands temporal diversity through Dirichlet-weighted inter-polation while preserving sequence structure. Experiments cover cryptocurrency, traffic, electricity, Electricity Trans-former Temperature, influenza, and weather data. QuantFlow obtains mean squared errors of 0.2834 on ETTm1 and 0.2218 on Weather, and a 20-client non-IID deployment retains use-ful accuracy after three communication rounds without cen-tralizing raw records. The results indicate that selective state-space modelling is a promising basis for scalable, uncer-tainty-aware, and privacy-conscious time-series prediction, while also revealing limitations on irregular epidemiological signals and long-horizon generalization.

</details>


### [117] [GRAFT: Grafted Reference Audio for Fine-grained Pronunciation in Zero-shot Text-to-Speech](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02633)
*Antonis Asonitis,Francesco Verdini,Aref Farhadipour,Vijeta Avijeet,Pierre-Edouard Honnet,Marzieh Razavi,Juan Pablo Zuluaga Gomez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRAFT是一种针对文本到语音神经编解码语言建模的逐词发音条件机制，通过短音频样本控制特定词汇的发音，有效解决罕见专有名词、外来词和技术术语的误读问题。该方法利用模型自身的语音分词器编码提示语音，并将其绑定到提示中的词位置，训练时通过语音转换分离提示说话人与目标说话人，确保输出保持目标语音特征。在盲听测试中，人类评估者认为GRAFT在难词发音上最接近参考录音，排名第一；在五种语言的客观基准测试中，其目标词音素错误率比仅依赖文本的基线模型降低22-39%，优于现有开源零样本系统，同时保持了说话人相似性和自然度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到语音系统虽具备高可懂性和自然度，但存在文本歧义问题，难以准确发音罕见专有名词、外来词和技术术语。即使采用音素条件模型，也缺乏对每个词发音的直接声学控制手段。因此需要一种能够精确调控特定词汇发音的方法。

Method: GRAFT引入一种基于短音频样本的发音条件机制，将目标词的发音提示以编码形式嵌入模型输入，使用模型自有的语音分词器对提示音频进行编码，并将其绑定至对应词的位置。通过训练阶段的语音转换技术，实现提示说话人与目标说话人的解耦，使得提示可来自任意声音，而输出仍保持目标说话人风格。

Result: 在盲听英语测试中，人类评分者一致认为GRAFT在难词发音还原方面表现最佳，最接近参考录音；在五语言客观评测中，目标词音素错误率相比相同文本基线降低22-39%，显著优于当前主流零样本语音合成系统（包括音素和文本条件模型），且在说话人相似性与语音自然度方面无明显损失。

Conclusion: GRAFT成功实现了对特定词汇发音的精准控制，解决了传统文本到语音模型在罕见词发音上的固有缺陷，在保持语音自然度和说话人一致性的同时，大幅提升了发音准确性，为高精度语音合成提供了新范式。

Abstract: We present GRAFT, a per-word pronunciation conditioning mechanism for text-to-speech neural codec language modeling. Existing systems reach high intelligibility and naturalness but inherit the ambiguity of text and mispronounce rare proper nouns, loanwords and technical terms. Even phoneme-conditioned models offer no direct acoustic handle for per-word pronunciation. GRAFT controls the pronunciation of a chosen word from a short spoken sample of it, encoded with the model's own speech tokenizer and bound to the word's position in the prompt. Voice conversion during training-data construction disentangles the hint speaker from the target speaker, so the hint may come from any voice while the output stays in the target voice. In a blind English listening study, human raters rank GRAFT first by a clear margin, judging its rendering of the difficult word closest to a reference recording of that word. On a five-language objective benchmark, GRAFT reduces target-word phoneme error rate by 22-39% over the identical text-only backbone and outperforms competitive open-source zero-shot systems, both phoneme- and text-conditioned, on target-word pronunciation, while preserving speaker similarity and naturalness.

</details>


### [118] [Federated Learning for Object Detection: Enabling Collaborative Drone Learning Without Centralizing Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02636)
*Daniel M. Jimenez-Gutierrez,Enrique Zuazua,Georgios Kellaris,Joaquin del Rio,Oleksii Sliusarenko,Xabi Uribe-Etxebarria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在分布式无人机系统中使用联邦学习（FL）进行目标检测，以解决数据隐私、存储和带宽问题。通过在KIIT-MiTA数据集上实现基于Sherpa.ai FL平台的联邦检测管道，实验表明，与单机训练相比，该方法在mAP@0.50和mAP@0.50:0.95上分别实现了52.89%和67.80%的相对提升，接近集中式训练性能，且适用于边缘设备部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在安全关键的无人机和边缘视觉系统中，需要高鲁棒性目标检测模型，但传统方法依赖于集中化航空图像数据，带来隐私、监管、存储和带宽挑战，尤其在分布式无人机部署中难以将数据上传至中心化基础设施。

Method: 采用联邦学习（FL）框架，在不集中数据的前提下，让无人机本地训练并协同更新共享模型；使用Sherpa.ai FL平台在KIIT-MiTA数据集上实现联邦目标检测流程，并与单机训练和集中式训练进行对比评估。

Result: 所提出的联邦学习方法在mAP@0.50和mAP@0.50:0.95上显著优于单机训练，相对提升分别为52.89%和67.80%，且性能接近集中式训练，轻量级模型YOLO26 nano可在资源受限的边缘设备上有效部署。

Conclusion: 联邦学习能够实现可扩展、高性能且隐私保护的目标检测，在无需数据集中化的前提下，适用于大规模分布式无人机群的感知任务。

Abstract: Object detection is a fundamental capability for AI-driven perception in safety-critical drone and edge-vision systems, including disaster response, operational security environments, infrastructure monitoring and defense applications. Robust model performance in such environments depends on large, continuously updated datasets. However, training high-performing detectors typically requires centralizing aerial imagery, which raises privacy, regulatory, storage, and bandwidth challenges. This is especially problematic in distributed drone deployments, where visual data is generated onboard and is often impractical or undesirable to transfer to a centralized infrastructure.
  In this work, we apply Federated Learning (FL) for object detection, enabling drones to improve a shared model while keeping image data local and private. We implement a federated object detection pipeline using the Sherpa.ai FL platform on the KIIT-MiTA dataset, and compare it with Single-drone and Centralized baselines using mean Average Precision (mAP) at IoU thresholds of 0.50 and 0.50-0.95. In our experiments, the proposed FL approach remains close to Centralized training while dramatically improving over Single-drone training, with the best lightweight model (YOLO26 nano), suitable for deployment even on very limited edge infrastructure, achieving relative gains of 52.89% and 67.80% in mAP@0.50 and mAP@0.50:0.95, respectively. These results show that FL enables scalable, high-performing, and privacy-preserving object detection across distributed drone fleets without data centralization.

### [119] [Post-Generation Curation of Synthetic Images via Homogeneous-Heterogeneous Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02637)
*Disheng Liu,Tuo Liang,Chaoda Song,Yu Yin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在固定生成图像池的情况下，通过选择信息量丰富的子集来提升下游任务性能。提出一种无需重训练、与生成器无关的筛选方法，通过平衡保真度与多样性，有效缓解现代生成器过度生成典型模式而忽略类内差异的问题。该方法在多个基准上优于现有数据选择基线，使用最多减少40%的合成样本即可达到真实数据性能，并在分类和分割任务中持续提升效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型虽能生成高质量合成图像，但其生成结果常存在结构偏差：过度生成每类的典型模式，忽视类内多样性。当前方法多依赖于训练或微调生成器，或采用轻量级后处理技术，具有生成器依赖性和高专业门槛。因此，亟需一种不依赖生成器调整、仅通过选择最优子集提升合成数据效用的新机制。

Method: 将每个真实类别划分为典型（Homogeneous, HO）和非冗余异质（Heterogeneous, HE）两部分；基于保真度-多样性准则对合成图像进行评分，奖励语义一致性，惩罚典型模式冗余；该方法为生成器无关，无需重新训练。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，该方法显著优于现有数据选择基线，在分类和分割任务中均实现接近甚至媲美真实数据的性能，仅需40%的合成样本；即使在经过任务微调的生成器基础上应用，仍能带来性能增益。

Conclusion: 后生成阶段的数据选择并非替代优质生成器，而是提升合成数据实用性的互补策略，可显著降低对大量合成样本的需求，同时保持高性能表现。

Abstract: Recent generative models can produce high-quality synthetic images, offering scalable training training data for data-hungry models. Existing approaches to exploiting this potential typically involve 1) training or fine-tuning generators, or 2) using lightweight post-hoc adaptation like prompt engineering or inference-time guidance, making them generator-specific and expertise-intensive. We study a complementary question: given a fixed pool of generated images, can downstream utility be improved purely by selecting an informative subset? The answer is yes. We show that effective selection must counter a structural bias of modern generators: they tend to over-produce canonical modes of each class while underrepresenting intra-class variation. Building on this insight, we split each real class into a canonical Homogeneous (HO) subset and a non-redundant Heterogeneous (HE) subset, then score synthetic images by a fidelity-diversity criterion that rewards semantic alignment while penalizing canonical redundancy. The method is generator-agnostic and requires no retraining. Across multiple benchmarks, it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art data selection baselines and matches the real-data performance with up to 40% fewer synthetic samples. The same criterion remains effective when applied on top of stronger task-tuned generators, with gains on both classification and segmentation tasks. Post-generation selection is therefore not a substitute for better generators, but a complementary mechanism for improving the utility of synthetic data.

</details>


### [120] [A Granularity-Aware EEG Feature Framework for Psychopathology Dimension Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02670)
*Haofan Cheng,Jingjing Hu,Jingrong Pei,Shuaiqi Fu,Meilun Shen,Shuai Fang,Meng Wang,Dan Guo,Jie Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种粒度感知的脑电（EEG）特征管道，将多尺度描述符组织为全局、区域和通道级别，利用健康大脑网络（HBN）队列评估了四种精神病理维度（p因子、内化、外化和注意力问题）在四种EEG范式下的预测能力。树模型与粒度平衡的特征选择在特定条件下表现优于传统方法，但效应量仍较小。所选标记的空间和频谱模式与现有神经生理学知识基本一致。在独立的PEARL队列上的探索性跨数据集验证表明，所提出的筛选原则在协议变化下仍具技术可行性，但不声称具有跨数据集泛化能力。总体而言，多尺度EEG特征包含微弱但可检测的精神病理维度信号，粒度感知选择可作为未来基于EEG表型研究的有用特征缩减策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏系统证据支持不同EEG范式和特征粒度层级下精神病理维度的神经生理相关性，且儿童精神病理异质性强，问卷评分可靠性中等，因此亟需一种更精细的特征分析方法以提升预测效能。

Method: 构建粒度感知的多尺度EEG特征管道，涵盖全局、区域和通道三个层次；采用树基模型结合粒度平衡的特征选择策略，在HBN队列中对四类精神病理维度进行预测建模，并通过可视化分析揭示特征空间-频谱模式；进一步在独立的PEARL队列上进行跨数据集初步验证。

Result: 在部分条件下，粒度感知特征选择与树模型组合显著优于传统方法，虽效应量较小，但信号可检测；所选特征呈现维度特异性空间与频谱分布，与已有神经生理认知一致；跨数据集验证显示方法具备一定技术稳健性。

Conclusion: 多尺度EEG特征包含弱但可检测的精神病理维度信号，粒度感知特征选择是一种有效的特征降维策略，适用于未来基于EEG的表型研究。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) offers a noninvasive approach for examining neurophysiological correlates of dimensional psychopathology, yet systematic evidence across EEG paradigms and feature granularities remains limited. Here, we develop a granularity-aware EEG feature pipeline that organizes multi-scale descriptors into global, regional, and channel levels. Using the Healthy Brain Network (HBN) cohort, we evaluate the prediction of four psychopathology dimensions: p-factor, internalizing, externalizing, and attention problems, across four EEG paradigms. Given the heterogeneity of pediatric psychopathology and the moderate reliability of questionnaire-derived scores, this setting represents a challenging feasibility test rather than a clinical screening scenario. Tree-based models and granularity-balanced feature selection showed promising improvements over conventional approaches in selected conditions, although effect sizes remained modest. Visualization of selected markers revealed dimension-specific spatial and spectral patterns that were broadly aligned with existing neurophysiological knowledge. An exploratory cross-dataset sanity check on the independent PEARL cohort suggested that the proposed selection principle remains technically feasible under protocol shifts, without claiming cross-dataset generalizability. Overall, multi-scale EEG features contain weak but detectable signals related to dimensional psychopathology, and granularity-aware selection may serve as a useful feature-reduction strategy for future EEG-based phenotyping studies.
